20/05/2022, 4:41 pm - Nadine: #include<iostream>
#include <algorithm> 

using namespace std;
typedef string ElementType;

struct node
{
    ElementType data;
    node * next;
};

class stack 
{
  public:
    node* top;
    int count;
    stack()
    {
        top = NULL;
        count = 0;
    }
    
    void push(ElementType x)
    {
        node* newnode = new node;
        newnode -> data = x;
        newnode -> next = NULL;
        if(top == NULL)
        {
            top = newnode;
            count ++;
        }
        else
        {
            newnode -> next = top;
            top = newnode;
            count ++;
        }
    }
    ElementType pop()
	{
		if(top != NULL)
		{
			ElementType x=top->data;
			node* tmp=top;
			top=top->next;
			delete(tmp);
			return x;
			count--;
		}
		else
		{
			//return;
			exit(1);
		}
	}
    ElementType peak ()
    {
        return top->data;
    }

};
int main() {
	string str;
	cin >> str;
	
	stack s;
	string curr_s = "";
	for(int i = 0; i < str.length(); i++) {
		if(str[i] == '/') {
			s.push(curr_s);
			curr_s = "";
		} else if(str[i] == '\\') {
			reverse(curr_s.begin(), curr_s.end());
			string top = s.peak();
			s.pop();
			top.append(curr_s);
			curr_s = top;
		} else {
			curr_s+=(str[i]);
		}
	}
	cout <<  curr_s << endl;

	return 0;
}
